2017. A copy of the press release is furnished as Exhibit 99.1 to this report. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify">In accordance with General Instruction B.2 of Form <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">8-K,</FONT> the information in this Current Report on Form <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">8-K,</FONT> including Exhibit 99.1, shall not be deemed to be &#147;filed&#148; for purposes of Section&nbsp;18 of the Securities
Exchange Act of 1934, as amended (the &#147;Exchange Act&#148;), or otherwise subject to the liability of that section, and shall not be incorporated by reference into any registration statement or other document filed under the Securities Act of
1933, as amended, or the Exchange Act, except as shall be expressly set forth by specific reference in such filing. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><B>Item&nbsp;9.01. Financial Statements and

 <BODY BGCOLOR="WHITE">

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="right">Exhibit 99.1 </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:13pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT
 COLOR="#666666">Microsoft Cloud Strength Highlights Fourth Quarter Results </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:4pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:9pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666"><I>Commercial cloud annualized revenue run rate exceeds
$18.9&nbsp;billion </I></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666"><B>REDMOND, Wash.</B><B></B><B>&nbsp;&#151;</B><B></B><B>&nbsp;July 20,
2017</B><B></B><B>&nbsp;&#151;</B><B></B>&nbsp;Microsoft Corp. today announced the following results for the quarter ended June&nbsp;30, 2017: </FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT COLOR="#666666">&#149;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT COLOR="#666666">Revenue was $23.3&nbsp;billion GAAP, and $24.7&nbsp;billion <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT COLOR="#666666">&#149;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT COLOR="#666666">Operating income was $5.3&nbsp;billion GAAP, and $7.0&nbsp;billion <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT COLOR="#666666">&#149;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT COLOR="#666666">Net income was $6.5&nbsp;billion GAAP, and $7.7&nbsp;billion <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT COLOR="#666666">&#149;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT COLOR="#666666">Diluted earnings per share was $0.83 GAAP, and $0.98 <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666">&#147;Innovation across our cloud platforms drove strong results this quarter,&#148; said Satya Nadella, chief executive officer at Microsoft,
&#147;Customers are looking to Microsoft and our thriving partner ecosystem to accelerate their own digital transformations and to unlock new opportunity in this era of intelligent cloud and intelligent edge.&#148; </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666">The following table reconciles our financial results reported in accordance with generally accepted accounting principles (&#147;GAAP&#148;) to <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial results. Microsoft has provided this <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial information to aid investors in better understanding the company&#146;s performance. Additional
information regarding our <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> definition is provided below. The <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures presented in this release should not be considered as a substitute for,
or superior to, the measures of financial performance prepared in accordance with GAAP. All growth comparisons relate to the corresponding period in the last fiscal year. </FONT></P>

<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP,</FONT> respectively. The tax rates reflect a $1.8&nbsp;billion impact related to the utilization of prior years&#146; losses from Microsoft&#146;s phone business that were not deductible in the years
incurred. As a result of this tax item, earnings per share for the quarter increased by $0.23. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666">Microsoft returned $4.6&nbsp;billion to
shareholders in the form of share repurchases and dividends in the fourth quarter of fiscal year 2017. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666">&#147;We delivered a strong
finish to the year with 30% growth in commercial bookings this quarter,&#148; said Amy Hood, executive vice president and chief financial officer at Microsoft. &#147;We will continue to invest in key areas that drive future growth for Microsoft and
our customers.&#148; </FONT></P>

constant currency), with the following business highlights: </FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666">Revenue in Intelligent Cloud was $7.4&nbsp;billion and increased 11% (up 12% in constant currency), with the following business highlights:
</FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="3%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT COLOR="#666666">&#149;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT COLOR="#666666">Server products and cloud services revenue increased 15% (up 16% in constant currency) driven by Azure revenue growth of 97% (up 98% in constant currency) </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="3%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT COLOR="#666666">&#149;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT COLOR="#666666">Enterprise Services revenue decreased 3% (down 1% in constant currency) with declines in custom support agreements offset by growth in Premier Support Services </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666">Revenue in More Personal Computing was $8.8&nbsp;billion and decreased 2% (down 1% in constant currency) driven primarily by lower phone revenue,
with the following business highlights: </FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

<TD WIDTH="3%">&nbsp;</TD>

<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT COLOR="#666666">Windows OEM revenue increased 1% (up 1% in constant currency), slightly ahead of the overall PC market </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

<TD WIDTH="3%">&nbsp;</TD>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT COLOR="#666666">Windows commercial products and cloud services revenue increased 8% (up 8% in constant currency) driven by annuity revenue growth </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT COLOR="#666666">Surface revenue decreased 2% (down 1% in constant currency) mainly due to product lifecycle transitions </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT COLOR="#666666">Search advertising revenue excluding traffic acquisition costs increased 10% (up 11% in constant currency) driven by higher revenue per search and search volume </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666"><B>Fiscal Year 2017 Results </B></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666">Microsoft Corp. today announced the following results for the fiscal year ended June&nbsp;30, 2017: </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TD NOWRAP VALIGN="bottom" STYLE="BORDER-BOTTOM:1px solid #000000"><FONT COLOR="#666666">&nbsp;</FONT> <P STYLE="font-size:2pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:1pt">&nbsp;</P></TD>
<TD VALIGN="bottom" STYLE="BORDER-BOTTOM:1px solid #000000">&nbsp;&nbsp;</TD>
<TD VALIGN="bottom" STYLE="BORDER-BOTTOM:1px solid #000000"><FONT COLOR="#666666">&nbsp;</FONT> <P STYLE="font-size:2pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:1pt">&nbsp;</P></TD>
<TD VALIGN="bottom" STYLE="BORDER-BOTTOM:1px solid #000000" ALIGN="right"><FONT COLOR="#666666">16%</FONT> <P STYLE="font-size:2pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:1pt" align="left">&nbsp;</P></TD>
<TD NOWRAP VALIGN="bottom" STYLE="BORDER-BOTTOM:1px solid #000000"><FONT COLOR="#666666">&nbsp;</FONT> <P STYLE="font-size:2pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:1pt">&nbsp;</P></TD>
<TD VALIGN="bottom" STYLE="BORDER-BOTTOM:1px solid #000000">&nbsp;&nbsp;</TD>
<TD VALIGN="bottom" STYLE="BORDER-BOTTOM:1px solid #000000"><FONT COLOR="#666666">&nbsp;</FONT> <P STYLE="font-size:2pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:1pt">&nbsp;</P></TD>
<TD VALIGN="bottom" STYLE="BORDER-BOTTOM:1px solid #000000" ALIGN="right"><FONT COLOR="#666666">19%</FONT> <P STYLE="font-size:2pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:1pt" align="left">&nbsp;</P></TD>
<TD NOWRAP VALIGN="bottom" STYLE="BORDER-BOTTOM:1px solid #000000"><FONT COLOR="#666666">&nbsp;</FONT> <P STYLE="font-size:2pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:1pt">&nbsp;</P></TD></TR>
</TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666">The current year effective tax rate was 8% and 14% in GAAP and <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP,</FONT>
respectively. The tax rates reflect a $1.8&nbsp;billion impact related to the utilization of prior years&#146; losses from Microsoft&#146;s phone business that were not deductible in the years incurred. As a result of this tax item, earnings per
share for the year increased by $0.23. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666"><B>Business Outlook </B></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666">Microsoft will provide forward-looking guidance in connection with this quarterly earnings announcement on its earnings conference call and
webcast. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666"><B>Webcast Details </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT
 COLOR="#666666">Satya Nadella, chief executive officer, Amy Hood, executive vice president and chief financial officer, Frank Brod, chief accounting officer, John Seethoff, deputy general counsel and corporate secretary, and Chris Suh, general
manager of Investor Relations, will host a conference call and webcast at 2:30 p.m. Pacific time (5:30 p.m. Eastern time) today to discuss details of the company&#146;s performance for the quarter and certain forward-looking information. The session
may be accessed at <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">http://www.microsoft.com/en-us/investor.</FONT> The webcast will be available for replay through the close of business on July&nbsp;20, 2018. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666"><B>&#147;As Adjusted&#148; Financial Results and <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> Measures </B></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666">During fiscal year 2017 and fiscal year 2016, GAAP revenue, operating income, net income, and diluted earnings per share include the net impact
from Windows 10 revenue deferrals. During fiscal year 2017 and fiscal year 2016, GAAP operating income, net income, and diluted earnings per share include restructuring expenses. During fiscal year 2016, GAAP operating income, net income, and
diluted earnings per share also include impairment expenses. These items are defined below. In addition to these financial results reported in accordance with GAAP, Microsoft has provided certain <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT>
financial information to aid investors in better understanding the company&#146;s performance. Presenting these <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measures gives additional insight into operational performance and helps clarify trends
affecting the company&#146;s business. For comparability of reporting, management considers this information in conjunction with GAAP amounts in evaluating business performance. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666"><I>Net Impact from Windows 10 Revenue Deferrals.</I> With respect to our <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measures related to
Windows 10 revenue, we believe these measures bridge investor information and minimize potential confusion during the brief period between the time Windows 10 revenue recognition moved from upfront to ratable, and the adoption of the new revenue
standard, when Windows 10 will again be recognized predominantly upfront. The net change in Windows 10 revenue from period to period is indicative of the net change in revenue we expect from adoption of the new revenue standard. </FONT></P>

<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666"><B><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> Definitions </B></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666"><I>Net Impact from Windows 10 Revenue Deferrals.</I> Microsoft recorded net revenue deferrals of $1.4&nbsp;billion during the three months ended
June&nbsp;30, 2017 and net revenue deferrals of $6.7&nbsp;billion during the twelve months ended June&nbsp;30, 2017, related to Windows 10. Microsoft recorded net revenue deferrals of $2.0&nbsp;billion during the three months ended June&nbsp;30,
2016 and net revenue deferrals of $6.6&nbsp;billion during the twelve months ended June&nbsp;30, 2016, related to Windows 10. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666">With the
launch of Windows 10 in July 2015, Windows 10 customers receive future versions and updates at no additional charge. Under current revenue recognition accounting guidance, when standalone software is sold with future upgrade rights, revenue must be
deferred over the life of the computing device on which it is installed. This is different from prior versions of Windows, which were sold without upgrade rights, where all revenue from original equipment manufacturer (&#147;OEM&#148;) customers was
recognized at the time of billing, i.e., upfront. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666">When Microsoft adopts the new revenue standard, predominantly all Windows OEM
revenue will be recognized at the time of billing, which is similar to the revenue recognition for prior versions of Windows. Microsoft reflects the recognition of Windows 10 revenue at the time of billing in &#147;As Adjusted <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">(non-GAAP)&#148;</FONT> revenue to provide comparability during the short period where Windows 10 will be recognized over the estimated life of a device, i.e., ratably, rather than at the time of billing. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666"><I>Impairment and Restructuring Expenses.</I> During the fourth quarter of fiscal year 2017, Microsoft recorded $306&nbsp;million of restructuring
charges primarily related to its sales and marketing restructuring plan. During the fourth quarter of fiscal year 2016, Microsoft recorded restructuring and related impairment expenses of $1.1&nbsp;billion, including $630&nbsp;million of asset
impairment charges which reflected the performance of its phone business, and $480&nbsp;million of restructuring charges primarily related to its previously announced phone business restructuring plans. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666"><B>New Revenue Standard </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666">In
May 2014, the Financial Accounting Standards Board issued a new standard related to revenue recognition. We elected to early adopt the standard effective July&nbsp;1, 2017, using the full retrospective method, which will require us to restate each
prior reporting period presented. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666">The most significant impact of the standard relates to our accounting for revenue from Windows 10
licensing as previously described. Additionally, for certain multi-year commercial software subscriptions that include both distinct software licenses and Software Assurance, we will recognize license revenue at the time of contract execution rather
than over the subscription period. Due to the complexity of certain of our commercial license subscription contracts, the actual revenue recognition treatment required under the standard will depend on contract-specific terms and in some instances
may vary from recognition at the time of billing. Revenue recognition related to our hardware, cloud offerings including Office 365, LinkedIn, and professional services will remain substantially unchanged. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666">We expect to share more information on adoption of the new standard in early August 2017. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666"><B>Constant Currency </B></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666">Microsoft presents constant currency information to provide a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> framework for assessing how our
underlying businesses performed excluding the effect of foreign currency rate fluctuations. To present </FONT></P>

<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666">
this information, current and comparative prior period <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> results for entities reporting in currencies other than United States dollars are converted
into United States dollars using the average exchange rates from the comparative period rather than the actual exchange rates in effect during the respective periods. All growth comparisons relate to the corresponding period in the last fiscal year.
</FONT></P>

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666"><B>Commercial Cloud Annualized Revenue Run Rate </B></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666">Commercial cloud annualized revenue run rate is calculated by taking revenue in the final month of the quarter multiplied by twelve for Office 365
commercial, Azure, Dynamics 365, and other cloud properties. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666"><B>About Microsoft </B></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666">Microsoft (Nasdaq &#147;MSFT&#148; @microsoft) is the leading platform and productivity company for the mobile-first, cloud-first world and its
mission is to empower every person and every organization on the planet to achieve more. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666"><B>Forward-Looking Statements </B></FONT></P>

<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="center"><FONT COLOR="#666666"><B>MICROSOFT CORPORATION </B></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="center"><FONT COLOR="#666666">FOURTH QUARTER FINANCIAL HIGHLIGHTS </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT
 COLOR="#666666">All growth comparisons relate to the corresponding period in the last fiscal year. Please refer to the reconciliation of our GAAP and <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial results in the table provided above for
additional information. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666"><B>SUMMARY </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT
 COLOR="#666666">Revenue was $23.3&nbsp;billion, up 13% year-over-year. The increase in revenue was driven by growth in Productivity and Business Processes and Intelligent Cloud, and a decrease in the net revenue deferral from Windows 10, offset in
part by lower revenue from More Personal Computing. Windows 10 revenue is primarily recognized upfront in the More Personal Computing segment, and the deferral and subsequent recognition of revenue is reflected in Corporate and Other. <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> revenue was $24.7&nbsp;billion, up 9% year-over-year, including an adjustment to exclude the net revenue deferral from Windows 10. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666">Gross margin was $14.9&nbsp;billion, up 18% year-over-year. The increase in gross margin reflects growth across each of our segments, including
the acquisition of LinkedIn, driven by higher revenue and margin expansion. Gross margin percentage increased due to margin percent increase in More Personal Computing and segment sales mix, offset in part by margin percent declines in Productivity
and Business Processes and Intelligent Cloud. Gross margin percentage includes a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">10-point</FONT> improvement in commercial cloud gross margin across Azure, Office 365, and Dynamics 365. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666">Operating income was $5.3&nbsp;billion, up 73% year-over-year. The increase in operating income was driven by higher gross margin and a reduction
in impairment and restructuring expenses, offset in part by operating expenses related to our acquisition of LinkedIn. Operating income included an operating loss of $361&nbsp;million related to the acquisition of LinkedIn, including
$371&nbsp;million of amortization of acquired intangible assets. Operating income also included an unfavorable foreign currency impact of 6%. Current year operating income was negatively impacted by the net revenue deferral from Windows 10 of
$1.4&nbsp;billion and restructuring expenses of $306&nbsp;million. Prior year operating income was negatively impacted by the net revenue deferral from Windows 10 of $2.0&nbsp;billion and impairment and restructuring expenses of $1.1&nbsp;billion. <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> operating income was $7.0&nbsp;billion, up 13% year-over-year, including adjustments to exclude the net revenue deferral from Windows 10 and impairment and restructuring expenses. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666">Diluted earnings per share (&#147;EPS&#148;) was $0.83, compared to $0.39 in the prior year. Current year diluted EPS was negatively impacted by
the net revenue deferral from Windows 10 and restructuring expenses, which resulted in a decrease to diluted EPS of $0.15. Prior year diluted EPS was negatively impacted by the net revenue deferral from Windows 10 and impairment and restructuring
expenses, which resulted in a decrease to diluted EPS of $0.30. <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-GAAP</FONT> EPS was $0.98, and grew 42% year-over-year, including adjustments to exclude the net revenue deferral from Windows 10 and impairment and
restructuring expenses. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666"><B>SEGMENT INFORMATION </B></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666"><B><I>Productivity and Business Processes </I></B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT
 COLOR="#666666">Revenue increased $1.5&nbsp;billion or 21%, driven by the acquisition of LinkedIn and higher revenue from Office. Revenue included an unfavorable foreign currency impact of 2%. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

licensed <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">on-premises,</FONT> reflecting a continued shift to Office 365 commercial. </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666">Operating income decreased $235&nbsp;million or 8%, primarily due to higher operating expenses,
offset in part by an increase in gross margin. Operating income included an unfavorable foreign currency impact of 3%. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

intangible assets. </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

acquired intangible assets related to LinkedIn. Gross margin included an unfavorable foreign currency impact of 2%. Cost of revenue included $403&nbsp;million related to our acquisition of LinkedIn, including $217&nbsp;million of amortization of
acquired intangible assets. </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666"><B><I>Intelligent Cloud </I></B></FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666">Revenue increased $723&nbsp;million or 11%, primarily due to higher revenue from server products and cloud services. </FONT></P>

<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT COLOR="#666666">&#149;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT COLOR="#666666">Operating expenses increased $60&nbsp;million or 2%, driven by investments in sales capacity and developer engagement. </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666"><B><I>More Personal Computing </I></B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT
 COLOR="#666666">Revenue decreased $140&nbsp;million or 2%, driven by lower revenue from Devices, offset in part by higher revenue from Windows, Search advertising, and Gaming. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT COLOR="#666666">&#149;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT COLOR="#666666">Windows revenue increased $103&nbsp;million or 2%, mainly due to higher revenue from Windows Commercial and Windows OEM. Windows Commercial revenue grew 8%, driven by multi-year agreement revenue.
Windows OEM revenue increased 1%. Windows OEM Pro revenue grew 3%, outperforming the commercial PC market, primarily due to a higher mix of premium licenses sold. Windows OEM <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-Pro</FONT> revenue decreased
slightly, outperforming the consumer PC market primarily due to a higher mix of premium devices sold. </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT COLOR="#666666">&#149;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT COLOR="#666666">Search advertising revenue increased $124&nbsp;million or 8%. Search advertising revenue, excluding traffic acquisition costs, increased 10%, primarily driven by growth in Bing, due to higher
revenue per search and search volume. </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT COLOR="#666666">&#149;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT COLOR="#666666">Gaming revenue increased $44&nbsp;million or 3%, driven by higher revenue from Xbox software and services, offset in part by lower revenue from Xbox hardware. Xbox software and services revenue
increased 11%, primarily due to a higher volume of Xbox Live transactions. Xbox hardware revenue decreased 29%, driven by lower prices and a decline in volume of consoles sold. </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT COLOR="#666666">Surface revenue decreased $20&nbsp;million or 2%, primarily due to a reduction in volumes sold, offset in part by a higher mix of premium devices. </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><FONT COLOR="#666666">Phone revenue decreased $361&nbsp;million. </FONT></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666">Operating income
increased $716&nbsp;million or 68%, due to higher gross margin and lower operating expenses. Operating income included an unfavorable foreign currency impact of 4%. </FONT></P>

<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666"><B>INCOME TAXES </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666">The
effective tax rate was (17)% for the current quarter, compared to 7% in the prior year. The current quarter effective tax rate reflected a $1.8&nbsp;billion impact related to the utilization of prior years&#146; losses from Microsoft&#146;s phone
business that were not deductible in the years incurred. The prior year effective tax rate reflected a favorable mix of our income between the U.S. and foreign countries, as well as benefits associated with distributions from foreign affiliates. The
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> effective tax rate for the current quarter was (6)%, including adjustments to exclude the net revenue deferral from Windows 10 and restructuring charges as discussed above. </FONT></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666"><B>OTHER INCOME, NET </B></FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT COLOR="#666666">Other
income, net, decreased $52&nbsp;million, primarily driven by higher interest expense and an increase in net losses on derivatives, offset in part by higher net recognized gains on sales of investments and an increase in dividends and interest
income. </FONT></P>
